border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">英汉这些“省事儿”发音的共同点和不同点</strong><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style=" margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center; box-sizing: border-box; "><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;text-align: left;width: 100%;padding-left: 1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;transform: rotate(0deg);-webkit-transform: rotate(0deg);-moz-transform: rotate(0deg);-o-transform: rotate(0deg);margin-left: -1em;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(253, 177, 89);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section><section style="width: 0px;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: 0.2em;border-left: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-bottom: 0.8em solid rgb(255, 255, 255);border-top: 0.8em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.8em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section style="margin-top: 0.3em;padding-bottom: 1em;background-color: rgb(254, 209, 109);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="border-width: 0.2em;border-style: solid;border-color: rgb(253, 177, 89);display: inline-block;width: 100%;margin-top: -1em;margin-left: -1em;background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="padding: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">闲着没事儿又给英专或汉语言专业的宝子们想到个可以一挖的论文题目：有关汉语与英语口语中“省事儿”词的对比和讨论。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">汉语方言中存在很多“图省事儿”的口语词汇。比如普通话中的“怎么”，天津方言会说“něn么”、把“用”说成ròng、“是吗”说成shà。“您们”说成“nèn们”是河南方言，北京人似乎也会用nèn代替“您”。东北方言中“干啥”会直接省事儿说成“干哈”，“玩意儿”会直接一个音发出说成“váng”。诸如此类，还有很多。感受一下便知，方言的发法明显都要较普通话更省力和简便。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">英语口语中也有很多图省事儿的发音现象。缩约，如it will若缩成it’ll，可少摆一个/w/的口型。许多连读击穿也是为了省事儿，如give him发成givim，give them发成givem，give me发成gimme...如此都可直接略过一些“麻烦”动作（图来自Sound foundations）。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">其他单词间的省略技巧，如cup o(f) tea，o(f) feeling等，可用同化、失去爆破等语音规则解释。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">英语单词里也有不少省事儿发法，如months发成mons、clothes发成cloz、asthma发成asma等等。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">可以列举并对比看看英汉这些“省事儿”发音的共同点和不同点。</p><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;box-sizing: border-box;">往期内容：</p><p style='max-width: !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;line-height: 1.2;padding-left: 3px;padding-right: 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: rgba(94, 169, 210, 0.6);padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(9, 9, 9);text-align: justify;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">1.annoying </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/əˈnɔɪ-ɪŋ/ adj.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">making you feel slightly angry烦人的;使恼怒的;使生气的;使烦恼</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It is without doubt the most annoying of all ． 这无疑是最烦人的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">2.behave </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/bɪˈheɪv/v. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">表现;表现得体;有礼貌;表现得…的</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He only behaves like that for effect. 他那样表现不过是为了哗众取宠。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">3.as if </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">(强调某物不是真的)好像…一样,仿佛,似乎;(表示判断)好像,仿佛,似乎;(表示类比)好像，仿佛，似乎</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I felt as if my heart had stopped. 我觉得好像我的心都不跳了。（心脏不是真的不跳了 与事实相反 所以as if后的时态要叠加个过去时 本来用一般过去时-&gt;过去完成时）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">She travels around the world as if money is no object. 她漫游世界，好像钱不是问题。（钱对她来说却是不是问题 as if后时态不变）</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">4.moral </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/ˈmɒrəl $ ˈmɔː-/ adj.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">道德的;道义上的;道德上的;品行端正的;有道德的n.品行，道德(尤指性关系方面);寓意;教益</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">He turns every subject into a moral discussion. 他把每个论题都变成了道德的讨论。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">5. present </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">/prɪˈzent/ vt. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">提出;把…交给;颁发;授予;提交;(以某种方式)展现，显示，表现</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Eight options were presented for consideration. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">已提出八项备选方案供审议。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">6. be looking to do 打算/准备/计划做某事</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">We're not looking to make a fortune. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们没打算大赚一笔。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;padding: 0px 3px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;vertical-align: top;margin-top: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">This time Polly took the lead. There was something in this room which interested her more than it interested Digory: all the figures were wearing magnificent clothes. If you were interested in clothes at all, you could hardly help going in to see them closer. And the blaze of their colours made this room look, not exactly cheerful, but at any rate rich and majestic after all the dust and emptiness of the others. It had more windows, too, and was a good deal lighter.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这一次，波莉一马当先，屋子里有些东西对她的吸引超过了对迪格雷的吸引。所有的那些塑像全都衣着华丽。如果你对服装感兴趣，会忍不住走近去着。经过了那么多空荡荡、灰扑扑的房间后，这间屋里服饰的光泽，虽说不上十分赏心悦目，但无论如何，都将屋子映衬得多姿多彩。而且，这里有更多的窗户，要明亮得多。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 前面的路被堵住了。也许出了事故。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 城里每天有很多交通事故吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 并不是很多。不过正在不断上升。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 请慢慢开，我们有很多时间。安全第一。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: The road ahead is blocked. There might have been an accident.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Are there many accidents in the city every day?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Not really, but they are on the rise.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Please drive slowly, we've got lots of time. Safety first.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It's out of the question to leave the country without a passport. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">没有护照是__________离开一个国家的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. unselfishly adv. 无私地，为他人着想地</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">-ly 表副词，通常缀于形容词后</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: border-box;">unselfishly</span></strong></em> when he helped her get the promotion.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">他帮她升职时表现得很<strong powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;margin: 10px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;min-width: 10%;max-width: 100%;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);border-bottom-right-radius: 0px;padding: 0px 5px 4px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);font-size: 18px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词汇补充</strong></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 5px 0% 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;font-size: 11px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-top: 1.2em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-left: 0.7em solid transparent !important;border-right: 0.7em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;text-align: center;line-height: 1;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-left: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: border-box;">Vocabulary</strong></p></section><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span><span style="width: 0px;display: inline-block;opacity: 0.6;border-right: 0.6em solid rgb(249, 110, 87);border-top: 0.5em solid transparent !important;border-bottom: 0.5em solid transparent !important;box-sizing: border-box;"> </span> </section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;color: rgb(249, 110, 87);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">请上下滑动查看</strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: center;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 100%;height: 240px;vertical-align: top;overflow-y: auto;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="overflow-x: hidden;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 20px 0% 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;border-width: 2px;border-style: solid;border-color: transparent;padding: 0.1em 0.3em;color: rgb(17, 1, 1);text-align: left;line-height: 1.5;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">preach 音标：/ priːtʃ / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to give a religious talk in a public place, especially in a church during a service</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：布道，讲道（尤指教堂中礼拜时）</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：She preached to the congregation about forgiveness. 她向会众宣讲宽恕的道理。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">choir 英音：/ ˈkwaɪə(r) / 美音：/ ˈkwaɪər  /  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：a group of people who sing together, for example in church services or public performances</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：（教堂的）唱诗班；（公开演出的）合唱团，歌唱队</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：She sings in the school choir. 她是校合唱队的成员。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">convince </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">音标：/ kənˈvɪns / </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义：to make sb/yourself believe that sth is true</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：使确信；使相信；使信服</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：You'll need to convince them of your enthusiasm for the job. 你要使他们相信你殷切希望得到这份工作。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I'd convinced myself (that) I was right. 我确信自己是正确的。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">property  英音：/ ˈprɒpəti  / 美音：/ ˈprɑːpərti  /  </p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义1：land and buildings</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：不动产；房地产</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：The price of property has risen enormously. 房地产的价格大幅上升了。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">英文释义2：a building or buildings and the surrounding land</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">中文释义：房屋及院落；庄园；房地产</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">例：There are a lot of empty properties in the area. 这个地区有大量的闲置房地产。</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">t </span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">for the kids, but for everyone! It coul</span><span style="text-decoration: line-through;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(0, 176, 240);box-sizing: border-box;">d</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> be a gathering place and a place for communit</span><span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: red;box-sizing: border-box;">y a</span></span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">ctivities.</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">这不仅对孩子们有益，对每个人都有好处！它可以作为聚会的场所以及社区活动的区域</span><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);display: none;box-sizing: border-box;">==dp@BOOKqAZWJBH49)6E*5Yz!Fk</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;background: white;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;"> </span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">I </span></em><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: Arial, sans-serif;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">already know all this!</span></p><p style="line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 16px;font-family: 宋体;color: rgb(40, 40, 40);box-sizing: border-box;">这些我都知道！</span></p><p style="text-align: left;line-height: 20px;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I can hardly describe the clothes. The figures were all robed and had crowns on their heads. Their robes were of crimson and silvery grey and deep purple and vivid green: and there were patterns, and pictures of flowers and strange beasts, in needlework all over them. Precious stones of astonishing size and brightness stared from their crowns and hung in chains round their necks and peeped out from all the places where anything was fastened.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我很难描绘他们的服装。那些塑像全部长袍加身，头戴王冠。绯红、银灰、深紫和鲜绿色的长袍上绣着图案、花卉和怪兽。大得惊人、亮得耀眼的珍稀宝石从他们的王冠和项链上进射出夺目的光彩，全身每一处有装饰的地方都闪耀着珠光宝气。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我绝不再跟他共事！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 怎么了？又吵架了？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 你能帮我把材料从他那儿拿回来吗？拜托！</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 别问我，我可不想卷进你们的争吵当中。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: I'll never ever work together with him!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: What happened? Quarrel again?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Will you take my materials back from him for me? Please!</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: Don't ask me. I don't wanna be involved in your quarrel.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It doesn't make sense to read such a boring novel.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">读这种无聊的小说____________。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">毫无意义</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><p style="text-align: left;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">今日发音练习重点：</strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">1. th</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">ough</span></strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">t/ɔː/和 l</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">o</span></strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">st /ɒ/元音不同；</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">2. Confuc</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">iu</span></strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">s /kənˈfjuːʃəs/不要发卷舌音；</span></strong></p><p style="text-align: justify;white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">3. peril</span></strong><span style="color: rgb(255, 0, 0);"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="box-sizing: border-box;">ou</span></strong></span><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(62, 62, 62);box-sizing: border-box;">s中的-ous不要发卷舌音。</span></strong></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-webkit-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-moz-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);-o-transform: translate3d(-10px, 0px, 0px);text-align: left;margin: 20px 0% 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;width: 40%;border-width: 0px 6px 0px 0px;border-style: solid;border-left-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);border-right-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);padding: 0px;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;background-color: rgb(161, 199, 135);box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;color: rgb(252, 252, 252);box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;">言之有物</em></p></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="text-align: justify;font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">1. labor lost对应原文中的“罔”。</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">“罔”是迷惑而无所得；译文中labor一词，强调了为“学”而付出的身体上的实际行动，强调“学”的动作；后接lost，表明“学而不思”是一种“白学习”的行为，就算一天24小时学习，没有思考的过程，也只是浪费时间和精力而已。</span></em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">2. thought n.</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→思想，想法；</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It’s an interesting <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">thought</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">想法</strong>很有趣。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→思考</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">lost/deep in <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">thought</span></strong></em></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">陷入<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">思索</strong>/在沉<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">思</strong>中</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→主意，观点（复数） thoughts on sth</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Any <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">thoughts</span></strong></em> on how we should spend the money?</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">关于我们该如何花这些钱，谁有什么<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">建议</strong>吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(18, 17, 17);box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">→关怀；顾虑</strong></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You are always in my <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">thoughts</span></strong></em> (=used to tell someone that you think and care about them a lot).</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你始终在我的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">心里</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="font-size: 14px;box-sizing: border-box;">殆：通假“怠”，精神疲倦而无所得，后半句意为：只思考不学习，就不能及时汲取新的营养，不能扩大知识面，也就不会是一个才富五车的人。</span></em></span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">3. perilous = very dangerous adj. 非常危险的</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">a <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">perilous</span></strong></em> journey across the mountains</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">穿越群山的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>旅程</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">The country roads are quite <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">perilous</span></strong></em>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">这些乡间道路很<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;text-align: left;">…considering the <em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">perilous</span></strong></em> state of the city of Houston, the state of everything.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">考虑到休斯顿的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>环境和现状。</p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin-top: 10px;margin-bottom: 10px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="max-width: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">现在，这个国家的经济陷入了严重<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危机</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>的局面。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"> </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgba(242, 70, 12, 0.92);box-sizing: border-box;">★原声例句：</span></strong>And we're <span style="text-decoration: underline;">at a <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="text-decoration: underline;color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">perilous</span></em></strong> point</span> in history.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我们正处于历史的<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">危险</strong>时刻。</p><p style="white-space: The <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;"><em style="box-sizing: border-box;"><span style="color: rgb(232, 39, 39);box-sizing: border-box;">peril</span></em></strong> was desperate.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：Look,I know you haven't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">warmed up to me </strong>yet, but I promise you will if you get to know me.  我知道你对我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">还没什么好感</strong>，但了解我之后一定会有改观的。  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"> warm (up) to/ towards XX  开始喜欢上XX；开始接受XX;  熟悉XX；融入XX;</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It took residents a while to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">warm up to him</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">居民需要一段时间来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">熟悉他</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, your mom's never been too thrilled with our relationship. Maybe I should get her something so <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">she warms up to me</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你妈妈一直对我们的感情不太感冒。或许我该给她点什么，让她能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">慢慢接受我</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Sweetie, sometimes it takes a while to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">warm up to people</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">亲爱的，有时候<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">融入人群</strong>中是需要时间的。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: So...perhaps we'll work together. But no, we won't be friends</p><p style="margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">E</strong>: It's tonight at eight. style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">原句</strong>：Look,I know you haven't <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">warmed up to me </strong>yet, but I promise you will if you get to know me.  我知道你对我<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">还没什么好感</strong>，但了解我之后一定会有改观的。  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">词链</strong>：<span style="text-decoration: underline;box-sizing: border-box;"> warm (up) to/ towards XX  开始喜欢上XX；开始接受XX;  熟悉XX；融入XX;</span></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句1</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">It took residents a while to <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">warm up to him</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">居民需要一段时间来<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">熟悉他</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句2</strong>：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">You know, your mom's never been too thrilled with our relationship. Maybe I should get her something so <strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">she warms up to me</strong>.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">你妈妈一直对我们的感情不太感冒。或许我该给她点什么，让她能<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">慢慢接受我</strong>。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">例句3：</strong></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">亲爱的，有时候<strong style="box-sizing: border-box;">融入人群</strong>中是需要时间的。</p></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="transform: border-box;"></section></section></section></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p></section><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 10px 0%;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;width: 29%;box-shadow: rgb(0, 0, 0) 0px 0px 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><section powered-by="xiumi.us" style="margin: 0px 0%;text-align: right;box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: top;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"><section style="display: inline-block;vertical-align: bottom;width: 10px;margin-bottom: 5px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(132, 132, 132);box-sizing: border-box;"></section></section></section></section></section><section style="text-align: justify;padding: 0px 20px;font-size: 14px;color: rgb(51, 59, 108);line-height: 1.8;box-sizing: border-box;"><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">美文</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">Polly nodded. All the faces they could see were certainly nice. Both the men and women looked kind and wise, and they seemed to come of a handsome race. But after the children had gone a few steps down the room they came to faces that looked a little different. These were very solemn faces. You felt you would have to mind your P's and Q's, if you ever met living people who looked like that. When they had gone a little further, they found themselves among faces they didn't like: this was about the middle of the room. The faces here looked very strong and proud and happy, but they looked cruel.  </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">波莉点点头。他们看见的所有面孔都很可爱。男男女女都显得聪明而善良，而且，似乎是一个漂亮、英俊的种族的后代。但当孩子们朝屋子中间走了几步后，他们看见的面孔便有些异样。这些面孔十分严肃，使你觉得，如果你遇到有这种而孔的活生生的人，便不得不注意自己的言行举止。又走了几步，眼前的面孔看去非常强悍、自豪、得惫，却十分冷酷，是他们不喜欢的那一种。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">对话</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 我可以跟我的朋友整晚在外吗？</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 不行。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: 但我们会小心的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: 那是不可能的。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: Can I stay out all night with my friends? </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: No way. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A: But we'll be careful. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">B: It's out of the question. </p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">专项</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">I thought I'd make a difference, but no one knows I'm here.</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">我还妄想____________，到头来还不是默默无闻。</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br style="box-sizing: border-box;"/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">大展身手</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: That would give mortals a shot at immortality and unite the Greeks in the process. </a></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">take place 的近义表达为：</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;">A  happen  B replace  C substitute</p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><br/></p><p style="white-space: normal;margin: 0px;padding: 0px;box-sizing: border-box;"><a data-itemshowtype="0" data-linktype="2" href="http://mp.weixin.qq.com/s?__biz=MzI4OTAyODUxNA==&amp;mid=2653553309&amp;idx=1&amp;sn=4befb2eca5dc68620119c4c60b8c9bd0&amp;chksm=f7ebc250c09c4b46e29d44a9ce9bd6022d22aba5127bd54e6d0b400dc352b30e144832f24434&amp;scene=21#wechat_redirect" tab="innerlink" target="_blank" textvalue="4.
